[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe project’s fuzz-testing harness reported a libFuzzer timeout when exercising the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mZIP decompression logic in ZipArchiveInputStream.  To prevent hangs during [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minflation, a contributor attempted to replace the simple `[0m[1;35minf.inflate[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minside `[0m[1;35mreadFromInflater[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, int, int[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with a retry loop that counts [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MAX_INFLATE_ATTEMPTS`, calls `[0m[1;35mfill[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` between tries, and aborts after too many [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mzero-byte returns.  After applying the patch, the build failed with eight [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompilation errors: redefinition of the local variable `read`, unknown symbols [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`off`, `len`, `inflater`, and `MAX_INFLATE_ATTEMPTS`.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzzing with libFuzzer triggered a timeout when processing certain ZIP streams[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvia `ZipArchiveInputStream`.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The harness code repeatedly called the stream’s `[0m[1;35mreadFromInflater[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod, and the inflation step could return zero indefinitely if no progress was [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmade, causing the fuzzer to hang.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Observations in the Initial Issue  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The timeout log simply reported `ERROR: libFuzzer: timeout` with no stack [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrace or exception.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Inspection of `[0m[1;35mZipArchiveInputStream.readFromInflater[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, int, int[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` shows[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma single call to `[0m[1;35minf.inflate[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer, offset, length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` inside a do/while loop that [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mretries only when `[0m[1;35minf.needsInput[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is true.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The contributor removed the original try/catch around `[0m[1;35minf.inflate[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroduced:  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • A declaration `int read; int attempts = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;`  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • A `while` loop:  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         while `read = [0m[1;35minflater.inflate[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer, off, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` returns [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, and the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minflater is neither finished nor needing input,  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         increment `attempts`, abort with `IOException` after exceeding [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MAX_INFLATE_ATTEMPTS`, otherwise call `[0m[1;35mfill[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The unchanged `do [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mread == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && [0m[1;35minf.needsInput[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` block was left[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min place after the new loop.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Compilation Errors After Patch  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `variable read is already defined in method [0m[1;35mreadFromInflater[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,int,int[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe patch redeclared `int read` although the method already has a `read` variable. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `cannot find symbol: off, len`: The patch referred to parameters named `off` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `len`, but the method’s formal parameters are named differently [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`offset`, `length`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `cannot find symbol: inflater, MAX_INFLATE_ATTEMPTS`: The patch used [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`inflater` instead of the existing `inf` field/reference, and introduced [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MAX_INFLATE_ATTEMPTS` without defining it.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Code Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Signature and existing locals of `[0m[1;35mreadFromInflater[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m b, int offset, int [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Definition or placement of a `MAX_INFLATE_ATTEMPTS` constant: determine [0m       [2m                [0m
